#Shipment origin,Shipment destination,1st terminal on path,2nd terminal on path,.....,6th terminal on path
#In notation of paper, these lines are
#o_k,d_k,v_1^{k},v_2^{k},\ldots,v_6^{k} although not all shipments have paths that are six terminals long
#as an example, line 4 (ABL,ATH) says that a shipment going from ABL to ATH follows the path ABL -> DLS -> ATL ->ATH
Origin,Destination,T1,T2,T3,T4,T5,T6
